    SELECT TOP(1) [b].[Id], [b].[BlogCategoryId], [b].[CreatedDate], [b].[Description], [b].[HighlightText], [b].[Title], [b0].[Id] AS [Id0], [b0].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [b0].[Name]
    FROM [BlogPosts] AS [b]
    INNER JOIN [BlogCategories] AS [b0] ON [b].[BlogCategoryId] = [b0].[Id]
    WHERE [b].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN [BlogPostImgs] AS [b1] ON [t].[Id] = [b1].[BlogPostId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0]
